 newjiland ko pakistan or australia ke khilaaf pichley do muqablon main haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa he

 aise main vah points teble main tisare number par pahunch jaaegi

 aise main use apni net ranret newjiland se behatar kerani hogi

 1

 net ran rate3
 Head to head match results 4
 toornament se pehle team kii variyataaise main isisi yah tay karegi ki koun si team semifinal main jaaegi

 jabaki, england ke 10 ank hi rah jaaenge

 agar england kii team newjiland se haar jaati he to uske 10 ank hi rah jaaenge

 use iske liye apane aakhri match main bangladesh ko haraana hoga

 2
 Jan Lokpal Bill: The Lokpal will have the right to investigate any complaint by the investigating agencies, including the CBI
 haalanki sabhi agenciyon par sarkaar kaa prashasnic niyantran hoga

 dilli lokapal bill:dilli ke lokapal ko jaanch ke dauraan adhikari ko nilambit karne ke saath hi dand dene kaa adhikaar bhi hoga

 1
 skin infections (skin Infection)-kai skin sambandhit samasyaayein aisi hai, jo kisi bhi vyakti ko ho sakati hai

 2
 Acanthosis Nigricans - This skin related disease mostly occurs in people suffering from obesity

 What the Finance Minister said on GST * It is under the constitution to decide the tax rate by GST Council
 * jiesti lagu hone se sabase bada phayda yah hoga ki desh main tex par tex nahin lagegaa, jisase vastuon kii keemat main ijapha nahin hoga
 * Center and states have vested their powers in a tax in the interest of the country, which will speed up development in the country
 * jiesti lagu hone ke baad desh main tex kii chori karnaa aasaan nahin hoga
 After the implementation of GST, the movement of goods and services from one state to another will be done without any interruption in the country
 * samvidhan ne desh main tex ke liye shaktiyon ko kendra or rajya ke bich suchi banaakar alag-alag kiya tha
 Now through the GST, the center and the state will collect tax together in the whole country

 * Stamp duty and real estate are excluded from the purview of GST on the suspicion of states

 Since the new Motor Vehicle Act came into force, there have been reports of rapid challaning of vehicle registration certificate (RC), insurance certificate, pollution under control certificate, driving license and permit certificate not showing immediately
 haalanki central motor whical rules ke mutabik agar aap trephic police ko maangane par fouran registration certificate (aarasi), insurance certificate, polution under control certificate, driving license (diel) or permit certificate nahin dikhaate hai, to yah jurm nahin he
 Supreme Court Senior Advocate Vinay Kumar Garg and Advocate Rohit Srivastava said that Rule 139 of the Central Motor Vehicle Rules provided that the driver would be given 15 days to present the documents
 trephic police tatkaal uskaa chaalaan nahin kaat sakati he
 This means that if the driver claims to show these documents within 15 days, then traffic police or RTO officials will not deduct the challan of the vehicle
 iske baad chaalak ko 15 din ke andar in dastavejon ko sambandhit trephic police yaa adhikari ko dikhaanaa hoga
 Advocate Srivastava also stated that under Section 158 of the Motor Vehicle Act 2019, the time for getting an accident or showing these documents in special cases is 7 days
 iske alaava trephic kanoon ke jaankaar lau professor dow rajesh dube kaa kahana he ki agar trephic police aarasi, diel, insurance sartificket, polution under control certificate, driving license or permit certificate tatkaal nahin dikhaane par chaalaan katati he, to chaalak ke paas court main isko khaarij karaane kaa vikalp rahata he
 Senior advocate Garg says that if the traffic police illegally deducts the challan, it does not mean that the driver will have to fill the challan
 trephic police kaa chaalaan koi court kaa aadesh nahin hai
 This can be challenged in court
 agar court ko lagata he ki chaalak ke paas sabhi dastavej hai or usko in dastavejon ko pesh karne ke liye 15 din kaa samay nahin diya gaya, to vah jurmaana maaf kar saktaa he
 Advocate Rohit Srivastava said that it is also necessary to have a witness sign in the challan

 lekin is baar sarkaar kaa kahana he ki vogurjaron ko paanch fisadi aarakshan bilase nahin, balki notification degi or ye notification jari karne ke power ke liye sarkaar aarakshan sansodhan vidheyak laaegi
